CREATE ({name:0})
CREATE ({name:1})
MATCH (v1{name:1}) MATCH (v2{name:0}) CREATE (v1)-[:Edge]->(v2)


MATCH (n)
  WITH collect(n.name) AS allNodes
  MATCH path=(s)-[:Edge*]-(t)
  WITH path, allNodes, [y in nodes(path) | y.name] as nodesInPath
  WHERE all(node in allNodes where node in nodesInPath)
  AND size(allNodes)=size(nodesInPath)
  RETURN path LIMIT 1
------

MATCH (n)
  WITH collect(n.name) AS allNodes
  MATCH path=(s)-[:Edge*]-(t)
  WITH path, allNodes, [y in nodes(path) | y.name] as nodesInPath
  WHERE all(node in allNodes where node in nodesInPath)
  AND size(allNodes)=size(nodesInPath)
  RETURN path LIMIT 1

MATCH (n)
  WITH collect(n.name) AS allNodes
  MATCH path=(s)-[:Edge*]-(t)
  WITH path, allNodes, [y in nodes(path) | y.name] as nodesInPath
  WHERE all(node in allNodes where node in nodesInPath)
  AND size(allNodes)=size(nodesInPath)
  RETURN path LIMIT 1

  MATCH path=(s)-[:Edge*]-(t)
  WITH path, allNodes, [y in nodes(path) | y.name] as nodesInPath
  WHERE all(node in allNodes where node in nodesInPath)
  AND size(allNodes)=size(nodesInPath)
  RETURN path LIMIT 1

  WHERE all(node in allNodes where node in nodesInPath)
  AND size(allNodes)=size(nodesInPath)
  RETURN path LIMIT 1

MATCH (n)
  WITH collect(n.name) AS allNodes
  MATCH path=(s)-[:Edge*]-(t)
  WITH path, allNodes, [y in nodes(path) | y.name] as nodesInPath
  WHERE all(node in allNodes where node in nodesInPath)
  AND size(allNodes)=size(nodesInPath)
  RETURN path LIMIT 1

  AND size(allNodes)=size(nodesInPath)
  RETURN path LIMIT 1
